< review>
I stumbled upon this magnificent eatery quite by accident when I deposited some mail at the adjacent postal annex and was hungry for any food. Up to now, Mexican food was an also-ran for me, because my European background caused me to prefer French, Italian and--Heaven help me--even German food. However, one most delicious meal at Lisa's hooked me for good. The efficient and friendly service makes eating there a real treat. For several weeks now, I have had lunch at Lisa's three times a week and was looking for excuses to eat even more often there.
I bet that you would leave from Lisa's place after a meal with similar positive impressions as I had. but it might be a good idea to hurry there for a delectable meal before this little jewel gets so popular that you have to wait a long time before you get served.
Rudy, aka Rudolfo< /review>

<Rate>4< /Rate><text>Five big stars.

Off the beaten path and tucked into a little mini-mall, but well worth the effort to find.

You can tell this place is quality the moment you walk in. It's clean and well-decorated with attention to detail and it also smells wonderful.  Friendly employees, too.  Another good sign.

We tried the taco salad with chicken, the carnitas burrito and the chicken taquitos.  Everything was outstanding.

Everything was also made to order.  You can watch them deep fry the tortilla shell for the taco salad and cook and cut up the roasted chicken while you wait.

The carnitas in the burrito were incredibly juicy and flavorful and the tortilla was fresh.  The chicken taquitos were enormous and tasted terrific.  We ordered a side of chips and those were fresh, too.

Even the salsas in the salsa bar were clearly homemade and delicious.

This is so, so much more than a taco shop.  In fact, it's not a taco shop at all. Aside from the Mexican food items, their strength is likely their roasted chicken dishes which we will try next time.

And there will be a next time.<//text>< Pictures>
None< /Pictures>

<Rate>5< /Rate><Review>This place is fantastic for lots of reasons, and let me tell you why -- at least from my experience.

I work in Rockridge in Oakland and was referred to Rockridge Optometry, where I made an appointment. The charge for the eye exam was going to be $235 out-of-pocket, since I don't need regular eye care and hence don't have insurance for eye care.

After making the appointment, I went online and started searching the best optometrists in Oakland and saw that Fruitvale Optometry was showing up at the top. And Rockridge Optometry -- while up there -- had a number of negative reviews.

So, I phoned Fruitvale Optometry -- who were very friendly and helpful at the start. I found out that the charge for an eye exam was $90.

WOW. That's NEARLY ONE THIRD OF THE COST of Rockridge Optometry -- where there were mixed reviews! And people seemed to love Fruitvale Optometry.

Given the positive review at Fruitvale, I decided to make an appointment there.

From the minute I walked in the door late (because I had some difficulty finding them) they were totally accommodating. The staff was extremely warm and friendly.

Omar did my initial tests and rated my old glasses. He was warm and professional, as you would expect in an appointment like this.

Dr. Luu did my exam. Again, warm and professional is how I'd describe our interaction. I'd also describe her as very smart and intelligent. I had lots of questions, as someone who hasn't done a lot of eye exams. She was extremely patient and took the time to enlighten me. She also identified for the first time that my left and right eyes were different. My previous glass prescriptions hadn't recognized that.

After the exam, Omar spent a lot of time with me recommending different eyeglass frames that would work for me, even though I told him I wasn't sure I was -- and at that point, I wasn't -- ready to order frames.

These folks are awesome. My hope is that more people from Oakland will find their way into Fruitvale to discover what I think is an incredible optometry group.<//Review><pics>None<//pics><response>None< /response>< GmapID>

< text>
Second time taking my vehicle to this repair shop.  The first time was for an oil change.

My vehicle was due to have the timing belt, water pump, and spark plugs replaced.  I researched approximately how much this would cost and then
went to Perlu to schedule an appointment.  The gentleman at the desk greeted me as soon as I walked in.  I told him what  I wanted to have done and he gave me an estimate which to my surprise was well below what I had researched.  I scheduled an appointment for the following week.

I dropped my vehicle off a little after 8am and was told it would be ready later that day or the following which was fine.  Later that afternoon around 1:30p I received a call informing me my vehicle was ready for pick up.  I was shocked!

I will continue to take my car here for future maintenance.  Their service is impeccable and the price point is great.< /text>

<Text>My partner and I started looking online at houses earlier this year.  I knew that home buying in CA was no easy task and wanted to meet with a realtor early on to educate us on the process (even though we didn't think we were going to be ready to make an offer for several months).</Text><Pictures>None< /Pictures><Resp>{'time': 1596998186114, 'text': "Hi Molly, thanks for sharing about your real estate goals in San Diego. We are still experiencing very low inventory for the number of buyers that want to buy a home and it is not unheard of to have as many as 10 of more multiple offers on a property. The positive is that interest rates are very low and had dipped under 3% interest depending on a buyer's credit score, amount of down payment etc. I checked my database and did not find your contacts, however feel free to message me directly and we can go over where you are at currently with loan approval. Many buyer's do not realize that they can use gift funds from a friend or family member if they do not quite have enough funds for a down-payment. If you were in the military and can qualify for a Veterans Administration loan (VA), there are 100% financing programs.  The two main other loan products would be the Federal Housing Administration (FHA) loan program where a buyer can qualify with putting 3.5% down of the purchase price. Then there are conventional loans which people think they have to have 20% down the purchase price although there are conventional loans that that a buyer can put down 3-5% of the purchase price. These loans have a Private Mortgage Insurance (PMI) fee on them because of the low amount of down payment to protect the lender in-case a borrower defaults on their loan. The good thing to know is this PMI can drop off a loan once the property has an acceptable amount of equity for the lender. I hope this helps explain some basic loan programs that are out there. It would be best to talk to a lender about what what loan programs would be best for you. I look forward to hearing from you so that we can discuss more when you have time. Warmly, Jason"}<//Resp><gmap_id>0x80d951a7ba9bd2ed:0x53e61674a68ef6ea</gmap_id></record></dataset><record>
